A great local candy and coffee shop with lots of really neat nick nacks scattered about for sale. Extensive flavored and unflavored coffee selection in 1lb or 1/2 lb options which you can get whole bean or ground to your liking.  They serve hot and cold coffee drinks, baked treats and have a few tea options. This place really feels like it belongs on some quaint small town Americana Main Street. This is a testament to both the owners and the dichotomy that runs through Simi Valley.</Text>

Disclaimer: I had a complex job involving a lot of parts.

I went to Perfect Auto Sound and discussed my job specifics and was reassured that the electrical work could be handled.
When I returned and discussed the specifics of the job at every step I was told it could be done.  When I reached a point that the representative felt he couldn't do he told me the whole job was too difficult and couldn't be done at all and to go to another shop.
I began by showing him the light and the instructions which I wanted connected above the driver and passenger side.  The light didn't need to be wired to anything other than power (I.E. the light did not need to turn on or off with the doors).  He said he could do it.
I was asking for a power line to be run from the battery to the rear of the vehicle which I was told could be done.
I asked for a fuse brick, which I supplied, to be connected to the power which I was told, with instructions, could be done.
Finally, I I showed him two additional lights that needed to be hooked up which but that's when I was told the job was way too much work and too complex and he couldn't do any of it.
Perfect Auto Sound seems to be good at window tinting. I saw him working on a tint job that looked really good but for any electrical work, big or small, I would avoid this shop.
I can't tell you if he was just confused in my original description of the work or if he uses deceptive sales tactics to get you to return to the shop but what I do know is that if your job seems even slightly too difficult he will just avoid the work all together.< /text>

< Review>
I've been listening to Dr. Puff's podcasts for the last few days, where he explores issues related to happiness: what it means to be happy and how to achieve contentment in life. The setup of his podcasts is simple (him speaking over what sounds like a faint excerpt of Bach's The Well-Tempered Clavier) but the format works amazingly well. The simplicity of the format means less distraction from the weighty themes he's wrestling with, such as the nature of happiness and how dreams relate to it. These are really soothing to listen to before bedtime and they've already given me food for thought about how to evaluate my life. Highly recommended for anyone out there who's reflective and wants five minutes of enrichment to start the day.</Review>

I listened to the 58 Happiness - Treating Life as a Permanent Vacation and I must say I really enjoyed it. I'm not too fond of podcasts, but Dr. Puff's podcast helped me realize a few things about how I view my life.

He talked about letting go of things - When we are attached to things, we get upset because we don't want to lose those things when things change. However, if we were to let go, we wouldn't get upset over the things that are not permanent.

Recently, I had a job interview that I have been wanting for the past 4 years. I finally got the interview, but I ended up stuttering and saying the wrong things. I got upset over this because I knew I did horrible. Now I realize that I need to let go of this interview and not be so attached because if not I will not be happy.

This podcast really helped me see things a little bit differently and now I definitely feel like I can be much happier.</review>

< review>
This cruise ship is not handicap accessible as they claim. My partner is in a wheelchair, and even though I called before getting on the cruise to confirm that there were handicap accessible ways to get on the boat/enjoy most of the activities/use the bathroom, the bathrooms were not accessible at all. Getting physically on to the boat was fine, but getting from the on-ramp area into the first floor cabin was tough. We had to really squeeze the chair through the door to get it in.

From moving chairs to sit at a table was fine, but the bathroom situation was the worst. There were two small single-stall rooms. The men's was completely inaccessible to a wheelchair, and the women's was supposed to be "handicap accessible". I informed the crew that I didn't think that a chair would be able to enter the bathroom and close the door, and they insisted that it would be fine. They asked if we would be able to fold the chair to bring it into the room..... to which I had to explain that my partner cannot use their legs so there is no option to fold the chair because they need to be in the chair when entering. They said that they could have the makeshift solution of keeping a further up door open, blocking view of the women's bathroom, and they could have the kitchen keep the galley door closed to give my partner privacy in case the door didn't close. I still didn't believe the chair would fit so I had my partner try to enter the women's room..... the chair didn't even fit through the door frame. Meaning that this cruise thought it okay for my partner to relieve themselves in a hallway?

So yes, you can board the boat in a wheelchair, but you'd need a bladder of steel during dinner and drinks to survive because the chances that you'd be able to use the bathroom are slim unless you have a child-sized chair. I am most disappointed in the poor expectation setting when I called, and the fact that the onboard crew insisted it would be possible to fit a wheelchair in the bathroom.

On a separate note, the food wasn't good. We rented out the boat and had a prefixes menu with four options. I can confirm that at least 3/4 were bad. The teriyaki salmon had a sauce that was sickeningly sweet. The prime rib seemed tasteless. The Portobello mushroom dish tasted like everything had been marinated in straight balsamic vinegar for days. On  positive note, The views of the lake were fantastic, and if you were able bodied this cruise would be beautiful. But don't come for the food. Come for the views only.</review>

Each time I place an advanced telephone order or order in person, there is always a long wait. Whether they are busy or not, average waiting period is a minimum of 20 minutes.

Keep in mind that all their proteins - whether it would be fish, carne asada, al pastor, or lengua are cooked in advance. All the cooks need to do is assemble these proteins for tacos, burritos, fries, etc.

So why the slow speed??? Both Alhambra locations are extremely slow despite my numerous complaints to the managers.

If you don't mind the lengthy wait or chaos at the restaurant, then Baja Cali is your place!< /review>

< Review>
I've tried the aguachiles tostada, fish tacos, carne asada tacos, chicken tacos, potatoe tacos, shrimp cocktail, asada sope, chicken sope, horchata, and cucumber water. I love the fish tacos the best. Their meat isn't lean, so if you don't like eating fat, you'll have to pick it out of your food like I do. If you like spicy foods try the aguachiles and get that cucumber water with mint and chia seeds. It's the most refreshing drink! A good meatless option are the potatoe tacos, they're delicious.
If you go on a Tuesday, the line goes all the way outside and it was way too crowded to eat inside because the fish tacos are 99cents each. On Thursdays the meat tacos are 99cents each.

*UPDATE* Feb 2018
I recently also tried the barbacoa tacos, piÃ±a agua fresca and strawberry agua fresca. All three were really good.  I gave it another go with the carne asada and chicken and ordered sopes but their meat still isn't clean so I couldn't eat 80% of it. I even ASK before ordering if their meat has "cuero". The cashier thought I meant skin and had me ask one of the cooks and he said it was clean (but it wasn't like always) -.- so I'll stick to the fish tacos and barbacoa!

*UPDATE* March 2018
Extremely lean meat in my sope!!! I ordered a carne asada sope and I FINALLY got no fat with my meat, it was delicious! I hope they keep it up!!!</Review>

<Pics>None< /Pics><user>115246144325654585948</user>< text>
Very tasty, reasonably cheap fish tacos.Nicely fried, flavorful, with tasty sides and sauce.  It seems like they have dollar fish tacos on Tuesday which I will for sure be coming back for.
I found that other items on the menu were closer to average. The pastor and carne asada tacos I had were both relatively tasty, but the meat itself didn't seem to be of great quality. The "crab" ceviche is actually made of imitation crab(I should have known from the cheap price). The strawberry agua fresca is delicious and not too sweet. Their condiment and sides bar is extensive, with radishes, onions, and large banana peppers available.

The service is just okay, and we had to wait a decent amount of time for our food.

Overall I would definitely come back and probably just order the fish tacos.</text>
